#Reworked for absolutism changes
estate_brahmins_land_rights = {
	icon = privilege_grant_autonomy
	land_share = 5
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.05
	can_select = {
	}
	on_granted = {
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		governing_capacity = 100
	}
	on_revoked = { absolutism_revoke_effect = yes } 
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0 #AI dosent use governing capacity
	}
}

estate_nobles_nobility_primacy = {
	icon = privilege_military_power
	land_share = 10
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	loyalty = -0.05
	can_select = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = no_other_mil_privilege
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_rajput_military }
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_maratha_military }
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		country_military_power = 1
	}
	on_revoked = { absolutism_revoke_effect = yes } 
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 25.2
		#AI wont pick this if its below 15% land or if its below 60% in age of absolutism or with influential estate
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_nobility_primacy }
			OR = {
				NOT = { crown_land_share = 15 }
				AND = {
					is_absolutism_active = yes
					NOT = { crown_land_share = 60 }
				}
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_nobles
					influence = 75
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			NOT = { mil = 3 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

estate_nobles_officer_corp = {
	icon = privilege_promote_purbias
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	influence = 0.05
	on_granted = {
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		general_cost = -0.25
		army_tradition_decay = -0.005
	}
	on_revoked = { absolutism_revoke_effect = yes } 
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 3.4
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			army_tradition = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			army_tradition = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			army_tradition = 70
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			army_tradition = 90
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

estate_nobles_levies = {
	icon = privilege_demand_more_troops
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } }
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	#Strong early game, declines to represent reliance on standing armies over estate levies.
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = { current_age = age_of_reformation }
		modifier = { global_manpower_modifier = -0.1 }
		is_bad = yes
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = { current_age = age_of_absolutism }
		modifier = { global_manpower_modifier = -0.2 }
		is_bad = yes
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = { current_age = age_of_industry }
		modifier = { global_manpower_modifier = -0.35 }
		is_bad = yes
	}
	influence = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_golden_liberty }
	}
	can_select = {
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_golden_liberty }
	}
	modifier_by_land_ownership = {
		global_tax_modifier = -0.10
		global_manpower_modifier = 0.5
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			has_government_attribute = free_noble_levies
		}
		modifier = {
			nobles_influence_modifier = -0.1
		}
	}
	on_revoked = { absolutism_revoke_effect = yes } 
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_rival_country = {
				army_strength = {
					who = root
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_idea_group = quantity_ideas
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = { max_manpower = 40 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			max_manpower = 200
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			estate_territory = {
				estate = estate_nobles
				territory = 50
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			estate_territory = {
				estate = estate_nobles
				territory = 40
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			estate_territory = {
				estate = estate_nobles
				territory = 30
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = {
				estate_territory = {
					estate = estate_nobles
					territory = 15
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = {
				estate_territory = {
					estate = estate_nobles
					territory = 10
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = {
				estate_territory = {
					estate = estate_nobles
					territory = 5
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { current_income_balance = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { current_income_balance = 0 }
		}
		#Shifting from estate levies to professional armies
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				current_age = age_of_reformation
				current_age = age_of_absolutism
				current_age = age_of_industry
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

estate_nobles_french_strong_duchies = {
	icon = privilege_french_strong_duchies
	loyalty = 0.1
	influence = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		OR = {
			has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_french_strong_duchies
			AND = {
				tag = FRA
				NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_strong_duchies }
			}
		}
		OR = {
			any_subject_country = {
				is_march = yes
			}
			vassal = 1
		}
	}
	can_select = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Art of War"
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = estate_nobles_strong_duchies_trigger_tooltip
				calc_true_if = {
					amount = 2
					all_subject_country = {
						OR = {
							is_march = yes
							is_vassal = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			vassal = 2
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		diplomatic_upkeep = 3
		reduced_liberty_desire_on_same_continent = 10
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
	   trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } }
	   modifier = { max_absolutism = -10 }
	   is_bad = yes
	}
	on_revoked = { absolutism_revoke_effect = yes } 
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = { #will lose it via invalid sooner or later
			factor = 10
			has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_french_strong_duchies
		}
		#Wants to revoke this for the disaster
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

estate_church_papal_emissary = {
	icon = privilege_send_emissary_to_pope
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		religion = catholic
		NOT = { tag = PAP }
	}
	can_select = {
		papal_influence = 20
		num_of_cardinals = 1
	}
	on_granted = {
		add_papal_influence = -5
	}
	penalties = {
		curia_powers_cost = 0.05
	}
	benefits = {
		papal_influence = 1
	}
	on_revoked = { absolutism_revoke_effect = yes } 
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_part_of_hre = yes
			is_emperor = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				tag = SWE
				tag = ENG
				tag = GBR
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = {
				reverse_has_opinion = {
					who = PAP
					value = 50
				}
			}
		}
		#Wants to revoke this for the disaster
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

estate_church_clerical_ministers = {
	icon = privilege_recruit_minister
	influence = 0.10
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } 
		} 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Common Sense"
				}
				NOT = { religion = protestant }
				NOT = { religion = buddhism }
				NOT = { religion = vajrayana }
				NOT = { religion = mahayana }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Emperor"
				}
				NOT = { religion = hussite }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Wealth of Nations"
				}
				NOT = { religion = reformed }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {

estate_cossacks_exploration_expedition = {
	icon = privilege_grant_new_world_charter
	land_share = 5
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.05
	
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_cossacks_exploration_expedition_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_terrain = steppe }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_cossacks_exploration_expedition_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_cossacks_exploration_expedition_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_cossacks_exploration_expedition_mod
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_cossacks_exploration_expedition_mod_revoke_tooltip
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_cossacks_exploration_expedition_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_cossacks_exploration_expedition_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_cossacks_exploration_expedition_mod_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_cossacks_exploration_expedition_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_cossacks_exploration_expedition_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 12.9
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 20
				has_terrain = steppe
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				NOT = { crown_land_share = 25 }
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_cossacks
					influence = 75
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_cossacks_exploration_expedition }
		}
		#AI wants to revoke for disaster
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

		}

	}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_dhimmi_lighter_dhimmi_taxes_privilege_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_dhimmi_lighter_dhimmi_taxes_privilege_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		church_loyalty_modifier = 0.05
		tolerance_of_heathens_capacity = 1
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 12.1
			NOT = {
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_dhimmi
					influence = 40
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1000
			tag = MUG
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}

estate_dhimmi_guaranteed_autonomy = {
	icon = privilege_grant_autonomy
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	loyalty = 0.2
	influence = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		any_owned_province = {
			NOT = { religion_group = root }
		}
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_dhimmi_guarantee_of_traditions }
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_dhimmi_guaranteed_autonomy_effect_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = dhimmi_tolerates_wrong_religion
		}
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = root }
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_dhimmi_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_dhimmi_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_dhimmi_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_dhimmi_guaranteed_autonomy_revoke_effect_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = dhimmi_tolerates_wrong_religion
		}
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_dhimmi_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_dhimmi_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_dhimmi_guaranteed_autonomy_revoke_effect_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = dhimmi_tolerates_wrong_religion
		}
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_dhimmi_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_dhimmi_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = { has_government_attribute = free_guarantee_dhimmi_autonomy }
		modifier = {
			max_absolutism = 5
			dhimmi_influence_modifier = -0.05
		}
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		#Muslim AI will actually convert again and only consider this privilege if it has low religious unity (eg indian sultanates)
		modifier = {
			factor = 1000
			NOT = { religious_unity = 0.5 }
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_dhimmi_guaranteed_autonomy }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1000
			tag = MUG
		}
		#AI will revoke this if its dominant religion is its primary religion
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			dominant_religion = ROOT
			has_estate_privilege = estate_dhimmi_guaranteed_autonomy
			religious_unity = 0.75
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 25
		#AI wont pick this if its below 15% land or if its below 60% in age of absolutism or with influential estate
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_jains_diplomacy }
			OR = {
				NOT = { crown_land_share = 15 }
				AND = {
					is_absolutism_active = yes
					NOT = { crown_land_share = 60 }
				}
				estate_influence = {
					estate = estate_jains
					influence = 75
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			NOT = { dip = 3 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

estate_jains_conscientious_objection = {
	icon = privilege_commission_jain_scripture
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	on_granted = {
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_jains
			loyalty = 10
		}
	}
	cooldown_years = 15
	loyalty = 0.1
	penalties = {
		global_manpower_modifier = -0.5
	}
	benefits = {
		interest = -2
	}
	on_revoked = { absolutism_revoke_effect = yes } 
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0.7
		#struggling with loyalty
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			NOT = {
				estate_loyalty = {
					estate = estate_jains
					loyalty = 30
				}
			}
		}
		#struggling with influence
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			estate_influence = {
				estate = estate_jains
				influence = 60
			}
		}
		#struggling with loans
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			num_of_loans = 10
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			num_of_loans = 15
		}
		#low on manpower
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			NOT = { manpower_percentage = 0.1 }
		}
		#court and country
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

estate_maratha_levies = {
	icon = privilege_recruit_from_marathi
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	#Strong early game, declines to represent reliance on standing armies over estate levies.
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = { current_age = age_of_reformation }
		modifier = { global_manpower_modifier = -0.1 }
		is_bad = yes
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = { current_age = age_of_absolutism }
		modifier = { global_manpower_modifier = -0.2 }
		is_bad = yes
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = { current_age = age_of_industry }
		modifier = { global_manpower_modifier = -0.35 }
		is_bad = yes
	}
	can_select = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_estate = estate_nobles
			}
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_levies }
		}
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_maratha_levies_for_muslims }
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			has_government_attribute = free_noble_levies
		}
		modifier = {
			maratha_influence_modifier = -0.1
		}
	}
	influence = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		NOT = { religion_group = muslim }
	}
	modifier_by_land_ownership = {
		global_tax_modifier = -0.10
		global_manpower_modifier = 0.5
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	on_revoked = { absolutism_revoke_effect = yes } 
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 10
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_rival_country = {
				army_strength = {
					who = root
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_idea_group = quantity_ideas
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = { max_manpower = 40 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			max_manpower = 200
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			estate_territory = {
				estate = estate_maratha
				territory = 50
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			estate_territory = {
				estate = estate_maratha
				territory = 40
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			estate_territory = {
				estate = estate_maratha
				territory = 30
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = {
				estate_territory = {
					estate = estate_maratha
					territory = 15
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = {
				estate_territory = {
					estate = estate_maratha
					territory = 10
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = {
				estate_territory = {
					estate = estate_maratha
					territory = 5
				}
			}
		}
		#Shifting from estate levies to professional armies
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				current_age = age_of_reformation
				current_age = age_of_absolutism
				current_age = age_of_industry
			}
		}
	}
}

estate_maratha_levies_for_muslims = {
	icon = privilege_recruit_from_marathi
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	influence = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		religion_group = muslim
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_maratha_levies_for_muslims_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = hinduism
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_maratha_levies_for_muslims_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_maratha_levies_for_muslims_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_maratha_levies_for_muslims_mod
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_maratha_levies_for_muslims_revoke_tooltip
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_maratha_levies_for_muslims_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_maratha_levies_for_muslims_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_maratha_levies_for_muslims_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_maratha_levies_for_muslims_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_maratha_levies_for_muslims_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		nobles_loyalty_modifier = -0.05
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 6
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				religion = hinduism
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = {
				manpower_percentage = 0.33
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

	loyalty = 0.05

		add_mil_power = -100

	penalties = {

	}
	benefits = {

	}
	cooldown_years = 5

estate_rajput_look_up_purbias = {
	icon = privilege_promote_purbias
	land_share = 5
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	influence = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		has_estate_privilege = estate_rajput_rajput_regiments
	}
	can_select = {
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_reform = governmental_purbias_register_reform }
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = look_up_purbias_upgraded
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = look_up_purbias
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = look_up_purbias_upgraded
			}
			remove_country_modifier = look_up_purbias_upgraded
		}
		else = {
			remove_country_modifier = look_up_purbias
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = look_up_purbias_upgraded
			}
			remove_country_modifier = look_up_purbias_upgraded
		}
		else = {
			remove_country_modifier = look_up_purbias
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 12.25
			has_reform = governmental_purbias_register_reform
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

estate_vaisyas_loyalty_privilege = {
	icon = privilege_royal_authority
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -10 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	loyalty = 0.1

	mechanics = {
		exempt_from_seize_land
	}
	modifier_by_land_ownership = {
		legitimacy = -10
		meritocracy = -10
		republican_tradition = -10
		devotion = -10
		horde_unity = -10
	}
	benefits = {
		merchants = 1
		range = 0.1
	}
	on_granted = {
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_vaisyas
			loyalty = 10
		}
	}
	cooldown_years = 15
	on_revoked = { absolutism_revoke_effect = yes } 
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		#low land share, low penalties
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			NOT = {
				estate_territory = {
					estate = estate_vaisyas
					territory = 10
				}
			}
		}
		#wants to maintain loyalty
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			NOT = {
				estate_loyalty = {
					estate = estate_vaisyas
					loyalty = 30
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			estate_influence = {
				estate = estate_vaisyas
				influence = 60
			}
		}
		#high territory
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			estate_territory = {
				estate = estate_vaisyas
				territory = 20
			}
		}
		#court and country
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

estate_burghers_patronage_of_the_arts = {
	icon = privilege_build_jain_temple
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	conditional_modifier = {

	}

	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = { prestige = 50 }
			add_prestige = 10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { prestige = 0 }
			add_prestige = 15
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { prestige = -25 }
			add_prestige = 20
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { prestige = -50 }
			add_prestige = 25
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = 30
		}
	}
	on_revoked = { absolutism_revoke_effect = yes } 
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = { prestige = 0 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = { prestige = -25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { prestige = -50 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			prestige = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

	icon = privilege_empty_throne
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -10 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}

		trigger = { ai = yes } #compensate for ai not using diet
		modifier = { nobles_loyalty_modifier = 0.1 }
	}
	is_valid = {
		NOT = { has_government_attribute = blocked_call_diet }
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = no_influence_from_diets_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { ai = yes }
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_nobles
				loyalty = 5
			}
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}

		can_give_agendas_without_interaction
	}
	on_revoked = { 
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
		custom_tooltip = no_influence_from_diets_tooltip_revoke 
	} 
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		#Good source of loyalty
		modifier = {
			factor = 12
			NOT = {
				estate_loyalty = {
					estate = estate_nobles
					loyalty = 30
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 12
			estate_influence = {
				estate = estate_nobles
				influence = 60
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0

		}
	}

estate_maratha_supremacy_over_maratha = {
	icon = privilege_empty_throne
	loyalty = -0.05
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -10 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = { ai = yes } #compensate for ai not using diet
		modifier = { maratha_loyalty_modifier = 0.1 }
	}
	is_valid = {
		NOT = { has_government_attribute = blocked_call_diet }
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = no_influence_from_diets_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { ai = yes }
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_maratha
				loyalty = 5
			}
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	mechanics = {
		can_give_agendas_without_interaction
	}
	on_revoked = { 
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes 
		custom_tooltip = no_influence_from_diets_tooltip_revoke
	} 
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		#Good source of loyalty
		modifier = {
			factor = 12
			NOT = {
				estate_loyalty = {
					estate = estate_maratha
					loyalty = 30
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 12
			estate_influence = {
				estate = estate_maratha
				influence = 60
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

estate_burghers_monopoly_of_textiles = {
	icon = privilege_monopoly_of_goods_cloth
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -10 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	loyalty = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		has_dlc = "Emperor"
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				trade_goods = cloth
				trade_goods = silk
			}
		}
	}
	can_select = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = unavailable_during_revolution_disaster
			NOT = { has_disaster = revolution }
			NOT = {
				has_disaster_progress = {
					disaster = revolution
					value = 1
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_disaster = french_revolution }
			NOT = {
				has_disaster_progress = {
					disaster = french_revolution
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					cloth = 1
					silk = 1
				}
			}
			add_mercantilism = 1
		}
		add_years_of_owned_provinces_production_income = {
			years = 24
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					trade_goods = cloth
					trade_goods = silk
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = MONOPOLY_INCOME_CLOTH_DESC
		}
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_monopoly_of_textiles_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trade_goods = cloth
					trade_goods = silk
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_burghers_monopoly_of_textiles_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_burghers_monopoly_of_textiles_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_monopoly_of_textiles_mod
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_monopoly_of_textiles_revoke_tooltip
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_burghers_monopoly_of_textiles_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_monopoly_of_textiles_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_monopoly_of_textiles_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_burghers_monopoly_of_textiles_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_monopoly_of_textiles_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	cooldown_years = 20
	on_cooldown_expires = {
		country_event = { id = monopoly_privileges.1 }
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = { #having the AI use these could lead to an unstoppable downwards spiral if it can't work out how to get rid of them
		factor = 0
	}
}

		custom_tooltip = estate_vaisyas_monopoly_of_textiles_revoke_tooltip

				has_province_modifier = estate_vaisyas_monopoly_of_textiles_mod

estate_vaisyas_monopoly_of_dyes = {
	icon = privilege_monopoly_of_goods_dyes
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -10 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	loyalty = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		has_dlc = "Emperor"
		any_owned_province = {
			trade_goods = dyes
		}
	}
	can_select = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = unavailable_during_revolution_disaster
			NOT = { has_disaster = revolution }
			NOT = {
				has_disaster_progress = {
					disaster = revolution
					value = 1
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_disaster = french_revolution }
			NOT = {
				has_disaster_progress = {
					disaster = french_revolution
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				dyes = 1
			}
			add_mercantilism = 1
		}
		add_years_of_owned_provinces_production_income = {
			years = 24
			trigger = {
				trade_goods = dyes
			}
			custom_tooltip = MONOPOLY_INCOME_DYE_DESC
		}
		custom_tooltip = estate_vaisyas_monopoly_of_dyes_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				trade_goods = dyes
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_vaisyas_monopoly_of_dyes_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_vaisyas_monopoly_of_dyes_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_vaisyas_monopoly_of_dyes_mod
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_vaisyas_monopoly_of_dyes_revoke_tooltip
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_vaisyas_monopoly_of_dyes_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_vaisyas_monopoly_of_dyes_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_vaisyas_monopoly_of_dyes_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_vaisyas_monopoly_of_dyes_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_vaisyas_monopoly_of_dyes_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}

	cooldown_years = 20
	on_cooldown_expires = {
		country_event = { id = monopoly_privileges.2 }

				trade_goods = silk
			}

		NOT = { has_estate = estate_vaisyas }

			NOT = { has_disaster = revolution }
			NOT = {
				has_disaster_progress = {
					disaster = revolution
					value = 1
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_disaster = french_revolution }
			NOT = {
				has_disaster_progress = {
					disaster = french_revolution
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					iron = 1
					copper = 1
				}
			}
			add_mercantilism = 1
		}
		add_years_of_owned_provinces_production_income = {
			years = 24
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					trade_goods = iron
					trade_goods = copper
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = MONOPOLY_INCOME_IRON_DESC
		}
		custom_tooltip = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_metals_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trade_goods = iron
					trade_goods = copper
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_metals_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_metals_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_metals_mod
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_metals_revoke_tooltip
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_metals_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_metals_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_metals_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_metals_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_nobles_monopoly_of_metals_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}

	cooldown_years = 20
	on_cooldown_expires = {
		country_event = { id = monopoly_privileges.5 }
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0
	}
}

estate_maratha_monopoly_of_gems = {
	icon = privilege_monopoly_of_goods_gems
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -10 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	loyalty = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		has_dlc = "Emperor"
		any_owned_province = {
			trade_goods = gems
		}
		NOT = { has_estate = estate_nobles }
	}
	can_select = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = unavailable_during_revolution_disaster
			NOT = { has_disaster = revolution }
			NOT = {
				has_disaster_progress = {
					disaster = revolution
					value = 1
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_disaster = french_revolution }
			NOT = {
				has_disaster_progress = {
					disaster = french_revolution
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				gems = 1
			}
			add_mercantilism = 1
		}
		add_years_of_owned_provinces_production_income = {
			years = 24
			trigger = {
				trade_goods = gems
			}
			custom_tooltip = MONOPOLY_INCOME_GEMS_DESC
		}
		custom_tooltip = estate_maratha_monopoly_of_gems_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				trade_goods = gems
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_maratha_monopoly_of_gems_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_maratha_monopoly_of_gems_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_maratha_monopoly_of_gems_mod
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_maratha_monopoly_of_gems_revoke_tooltip
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_maratha_monopoly_of_gems_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_maratha_monopoly_of_gems_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_maratha_monopoly_of_gems_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_maratha_monopoly_of_gems_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_maratha_monopoly_of_gems_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	cooldown_years = 20
	on_cooldown_expires = {
		country_event = { id = monopoly_privileges.7 }
	}

		factor = 0
	}

		custom_tooltip = estate_cossacks_prime_herding_rights_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_terrain = steppe
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_cossacks_prime_herding_rights_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_cossacks_prime_herding_rights_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_cossacks_prime_herding_rights_mod
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_cossacks_prime_herding_rights_mod_revoke_tooltip
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_cossacks_prime_herding_rights_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_cossacks_prime_herding_rights_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_cossacks_prime_herding_rights_mod_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_cossacks_prime_herding_rights_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_cossacks_prime_herding_rights_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { manpower_percentage = 0.1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = { manpower_percentage = 0.2 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = { manpower_percentage = 0.3 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 20
				has_terrain = steppe
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 30
				has_terrain = steppe
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_absolutism_active = yes #tax less relevant
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

estate_nobles_strong_duchies = {
	icon = privilege_royal_authority
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -10 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	influence = 0.1
	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		OR = {
			any_subject_country = {
				is_march = yes
			}
			vassal = 1
		}
		NOT = { 
		   	OR = {
		      	has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_french_strong_duchies
		      	has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_wattasid_viziers
				has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_lithuanian_strong_duchies
				has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_timurid_leadership
				AND = {
					has_ruler = "Shah Rukh"
					tag = TIM
				}
		      	AND = {
					tag = FRA
					NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_strong_duchies }
			  	} 
		   	}
		}
	}
	can_select = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Art of War"
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = estate_nobles_strong_duchies_trigger_tooltip
				calc_true_if = {
					amount = 2
					all_subject_country = {
						OR = {
							is_march = yes
							is_vassal = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			vassal = 2
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
		diplomatic_upkeep = 2
		reduced_liberty_desire = 10
	}
	on_revoked = { absolutism_revoke_effect = yes } 
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = { #will lose it via invalid sooner or later
			factor = 12
			has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_strong_duchies
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 15
			calc_true_if = {
				amount = 3
				all_subject_country = {
					liberty_desire = 50
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

estate_nobles_golden_liberty = {
	icon = privilege_golden_liberty
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } 
		} 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -15 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	influence = 0.15
	loyalty = -0.1
	is_valid = {
		OR = {
			has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_golden_liberty #Poland starts with it
			has_reform = elective_monarchy
		}
		government = monarchy
	}
	modifier_by_land_ownership = {
		global_tax_modifier = -0.25
		global_manpower_modifier = 0.5
	}
	can_revoke = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = PLC
					AND = {
						tag = POL
						NOT = { exists = PLC }
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_reform = elective_monarchy }
				is_year = 1600
			}
		}
		stability = 2
		has_regency = no
		absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes
	}
	on_revoked = {
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_estate = estate_nobles }
			add_stability = -3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = PLC
					AND = {
						tag = POL
						NOT = { exists = PLC }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_nieszawa_privileges
				}
				remove_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_nieszawa_privileges
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_pacta_conventa
				}
				remove_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_pacta_conventa
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = pol_zebrzydowski_rebellion_flag }
					is_year = 1600
					government = monarchy
				}
				set_country_flag = pol_pact_conventa_flag
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = { 
					has_reform = elective_monarchy
					has_reform = polish_elective_monarchy
				}
				has_estate = estate_nobles
			}
			country_event = { id = estate_privileges_and_agendas_events.1 }
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		manpower_recovery_speed = -0.10
		reinforce_cost_modifier = 0.1
	}
	mechanics = {
		exempt_from_seize_land
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0
	}
}

				name = estate_burghers_the_great_privilege_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_burghers_the_great_privilege_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_the_great_privilege_mod
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {

	}
	on_revoked_province = {

			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_the_great_privilege_mod

	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_the_great_privilege_revoke_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_burghers_the_great_privilege_mod

		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_exclusive_trade_rights_revoke_tooltip
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_exclusive_trade_rights_mod
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_exclusive_trade_rights_revoke_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_exclusive_trade_rights_mod
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 7
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = { num_of_cities = 10 } #would benefit smaller guys more
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			has_idea_group = economic_ideas
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

estate_church_for_the_faith = {
	icon = privilege_recruit_inouisitor
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		OR = {
			has_dlc = "Emperor"
			has_dlc = "Lions of the North"
		}
		NOT = { has_harmony = yes }
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = improved_expansionist_zealotry
			any_known_country = {
				NOT = { religion = root }
			}
			has_country_modifier = recently_force_converted_protagonist_timer
			has_country_modifier = recently_annexed_other_religion_timer
		}
	}
	can_select = {
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = improved_expansionist_zealotry
			any_known_country = {
				NOT = { religion = root }
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_church_inwards_perfection }
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_for_the_faith_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_for_the_faith_effect_tooltip
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			any_known_country = {
				NOT = { religion = root }
				war_with = root
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = improved_expansionist_zealotry }
		}
		modifier = {
			church_loyalty_modifier = 0.1
			land_morale = 0.05
		}
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			any_known_country = {
				NOT = { religion = root }
				war_with = root
			}
			has_country_flag = improved_expansionist_zealotry
		}
		modifier = {
			land_morale = 0.1
			church_loyalty_modifier = 0.1
		}
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_known_country = {
					NOT = { religion = root }
					OR = {
						war_with = root
						truce_with = root
					}
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = recently_force_converted_protagonist_timer }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = recently_annexed_other_religion_timer }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = improved_expansionist_zealotry }
		}
		modifier = {
			church_loyalty_modifier = -0.1
			land_morale = -0.05
		}
		is_bad = yes
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			any_neighbor_country = {
				NOT = { religion = ROOT }
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				is_at_war = yes
				overextension_percentage = 0.01
				revanchism = 1
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2 #small religion
			NOT = {
				calc_true_if = {
					amount = 5
					all_known_country = {
						religion = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

			share = -20
		}
	}

		factor = 0 #bad
	}

estate_nobles_statutory_rights = {
	icon = privilege_grant_autonomy
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	influence = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_statutory_rights
	}
	on_granted = {
		set_country_flag = statutory_rights_fl
		change_estate_land_share = {
			estate = all
			share = -30
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		min_autonomy = 25
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	on_revoked = { 
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
		clr_country_flag = statutory_rights_fl 
	} 
	can_revoke = { 
		absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes 
		if = {
			limit = { ai = no }
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = statutory_rights_20_years_tt
				had_country_flag = {
					flag = statutory_rights_fl
					days = 7300 #20 years
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = statutory_rights_10_years_tt
				had_country_flag = {
					flag = statutory_rights_fl
					days = 3650 #10 years (ai)
				}
			}
		}
	} 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0
	}
}

		set_country_flag = statutory_rights_fl
	}
	penalties = {
		min_autonomy = 25
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	on_revoked = { 
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
		clr_country_flag = statutory_rights_fl 
	} 
	can_revoke = { 
		absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes 
		if = {
			limit = { ai = no }
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = statutory_rights_20_years_tt
				had_country_flag = {
					flag = statutory_rights_fl
					days = 7300 #20 years
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = statutory_rights_10_years_tt
				had_country_flag = {
					flag = statutory_rights_fl
					days = 3650 #10 years (ai)
				}
			}
		}
	} 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0
	}
}

		}

				duration = -1
			}

				has_province_modifier = estate_brahmins_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_brahmins_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {

		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {

			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_brahmins_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_brahmins_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_brahmins_guaranteed_autonomy_revoke_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_brahmins_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_brahmins_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 1000
			NOT = { religious_unity = 0.5 }
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_church_brahmins_at_court }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			dominant_religion = ROOT
			has_estate_privilege = estate_church_brahmins_at_court
			religious_unity = 0.75
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				has_disaster = court_and_country
				has_country_flag = failed_court_and_country
			}
		}
	}
}

estate_church_one_faith_one_culture = {
	icon = privilege_one_faith_one_culture
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	influence = 0.1
	loyalty = 0.1
	land_share = 5
	is_valid = {
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_brahmins_one_faith_one_culture }
	}
	can_select = {
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_one_faith_one_culture_gta
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_one_faith_one_culture_gtb
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					religion = ROOT
					AND = {
						religion = THIS
						owner = {
							has_harmonized_with = PREV
						}
					}
					AND = {
						religion = THIS
						owner = {
							secondary_religion = PREV
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
					culture_group = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_church_united_faith_and_culture
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_united_faith_and_culture
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_united_faith_and_culture
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { culture_group = ROOT }
				has_owner_accepted_culture = no
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_church_false_culture
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_false_culture
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_false_culture
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_one_faith_one_culture_rta
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_one_faith_one_culture_rtb
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_united_faith_and_culture
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_united_faith_and_culture
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_false_culture
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_false_culture
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_one_faith_one_culture_rta
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_one_faith_one_culture_rtb
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_united_faith_and_culture
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_united_faith_and_culture
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_false_culture
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_false_culture
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		tolerance_heathen = -2
		tolerance_heretic = -2
	}
	benefits = {
		global_missionary_strength = 0.01
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = { has_government_attribute = free_religious_culture }
		modifier = {
			church_influence_modifier = -0.2
		}
	}
	cooldown_years = 15
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 12
			OR = {
				#dont bother with this unless you have access crownland
				AND = {
					NOT = { is_absolutism_active = yes }
					NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_church_one_faith_one_culture }
					crown_land_share = 25
				}
				AND = {
					is_absolutism_active = yes
					NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_church_one_faith_one_culture }
					crown_land_share = 55
				}
				has_estate_privilege = estate_church_one_faith_one_culture
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			tag = MUG
		}
	}
}

estate_brahmins_one_faith_one_culture = {
	icon = privilege_one_faith_one_culture
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	influence = 0.1
	loyalty = 0.1
	land_share = 5
	is_valid = {
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_church_one_faith_one_culture }
	}
	can_select = {
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_one_faith_one_culture_gta
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_one_faith_one_culture_gtb
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					religion = ROOT
					AND = {
						religion = THIS
						owner = {
							has_harmonized_with = PREV
						}
					}
					AND = {
						religion = THIS
						owner = {
							secondary_religion = PREV
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
					culture_group = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_church_united_faith_and_culture
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_united_faith_and_culture
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_united_faith_and_culture
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { culture_group = ROOT }
				has_owner_accepted_culture = no
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_church_false_culture
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_false_culture
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_false_culture
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_one_faith_one_culture_rta
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_one_faith_one_culture_rtb
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_united_faith_and_culture
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_united_faith_and_culture
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_false_culture
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_false_culture
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_one_faith_one_culture_rta
		custom_tooltip = estate_church_one_faith_one_culture_rtb
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_united_faith_and_culture
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_united_faith_and_culture
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_church_false_culture
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_church_false_culture
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		tolerance_heathen = -2
		tolerance_heretic = -2
	}
	benefits = {
		global_missionary_strength = 0.01
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = { has_government_attribute = free_religious_culture }
		modifier = {
			brahmins_other_influence_modifier = -0.2
		}
	}
	cooldown_years = 15
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 12
			OR = {
				#dont bother with this unless you have access crownland
				AND = {
					NOT = { is_absolutism_active = yes }
					NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_brahmins_one_faith_one_culture }
					crown_land_share = 25
				}
				AND = {
					is_absolutism_active = yes
					NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_brahmins_one_faith_one_culture }
					crown_land_share = 55
				}
				has_estate_privilege = estate_brahmins_one_faith_one_culture
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

estate_nobles_neighbor_raids = {
	icon = privilege_demand_more_troops
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -10 } 
		is_bad = yes

	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = {

			capital_scope = { continent = africa }
			technology_group = indonesian
			has_global_modifier_value = {
				which = may_perform_slave_raid
				value = 1
			}
			has_global_modifier_value = {
				which = may_perform_slave_raid_on_same_religion
				value = 1
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_nomadic_tribes_neighbor_raids }
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_maratha_neighbor_raids }

	}
	on_invalid = {

	}
	penalties = {

	}
	benefits = {
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 20
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes

		}

		}

	ai_will_do = {

			factor = 100
			has_government_attribute = no_influence_from_fetishist_privileges

			factor = 0

				AND = {
					NOT = { is_absolutism_active = yes }
					NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_church_patronize_foreign_cults }
					NOT = { crown_land_share = 20 }
				}
				AND = {
					is_absolutism_active = yes
					NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_church_patronize_foreign_cults }
					NOT = { crown_land_share = 60 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}

	icon = privilege_singular_cult
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	influence = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		religion = shamanism
		has_dlc = "Rights of Man"
	}
	can_select = {
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_church_flexible_cults }
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_church_patronize_foreign_cults }
	}
	on_granted = {
		enable_primary_cult = yes
	}
	on_revoked = {
		disable_primary_cult = yes
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_invalid = {
		disable_primary_cult = yes
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = { has_government_attribute = no_influence_from_fetishist_privileges }
		modifier = {
			church_influence_modifier = -0.1
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 100
			#i wouldnt say the other ones are actively worth pursuing to stack
			OR = {
				has_unlocked_cult = mwari_cult #discipline
				has_unlocked_cult = south_central_american_cult #morale
				has_unlocked_cult = zoroastrian_cult #fire damage
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

estate_burghers_control_over_the_mint = {
	icon = privilege_gold_mint
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -30 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	influence = 0.05
	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		gold = 1
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_vaisyas_control_over_the_mint }
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_jains_control_over_the_mint }
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_mint_mining_rights }
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_vaisyas_mint_mining_rights }
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_jains_mint_mining_rights }
	}
	can_select = {
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_control_over_the_mint_gt
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				trade_goods = gold
			}
			add_province_modifier = {

		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	influence = 0.1
	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		has_unlocked_estate_privilege = { estate_privilege = estate_nobles_carolean_march }
	}
	can_select = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = estate_did_not_have_carolean_privilege_for_five_years
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = picked_carolean_privilege }
				had_country_flag = {
					flag = picked_carolean_privilege
					days = 1825
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Cradle of Civilization" }
			army_professionalism = 0.4
		}
		army_tradition = 30
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_carolean_charge }
			remove_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_carolean_charge
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = picked_carolean_privilege
			set_country_flag = picked_carolean_privilege
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = estate_nobles_carolean_march_modifier
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		remove_country_modifier = estate_nobles_carolean_march_modifier
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_invalid = {
		remove_country_modifier = estate_nobles_carolean_march_modifier
	}
	penalties = {
		amount_of_carolean = -0.1
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes }
	cooldown_years = 5
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0 #ai dosent use caroleans so this needs to be changed around..
	}
}

		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		remove_country_modifier = estate_nobles_carolean_charge_modifier
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_invalid = {
		remove_country_modifier = estate_nobles_carolean_charge_modifier
	}
	penalties = {
		amount_of_carolean = -0.1
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	cooldown_years = 5
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes }
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0 #ai dosent use caroleans so this needs to be changed around..
	}
}

########################################

# Highlands Terrain

estate_burghers_mountain_expansion = {
	icon = privilege_dev_cost_mountain
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -10 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	influence = 0.1
	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_mountain_expansion }
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = mountain
					has_terrain = highlands
					has_terrain = hills
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_vaisyas_mountain_expansion }
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_jains_mountain_expansion }
	}
	can_select = {
		capital_scope = {
			development = 30
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}
		}
		num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
			value = 10
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}
			num_of_times_improved = 5
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_mountain_expansion_gt
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = mountain
					has_terrain = highlands
					has_terrain = hills
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_burghers_mountain_expansion_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_mountain_expansion_rt
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_mountain_expansion_mod
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_mountain_expansion_mod
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes }
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100 #might as well use it if you meet the requirements
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

					has_terrain = forest

# Tropical Climate

estate_burghers_tropical_nation = {
	icon = privilege_grant_new_world_charter
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.1
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } }
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -10 }
	}
	is_valid = {
		any_owned_province = {
			has_climate = tropical
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_tropical_nation }
			capital_scope = { has_climate = tropical }
		}
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_vaisyas_tropical_nation }
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_jains_tropical_nation }
	}
	can_select = {
		capital_scope = {
			has_climate = tropical
			development = 30
		}
		num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
			value = 10
			has_climate = tropical
			num_of_times_improved = 5
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_tropical_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_climate = tropical
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_burghers_tropical_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_tropical_revoke_effect_tooltip
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_tropical_mod
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_tropical_revoke_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_tropical_mod
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100 #might as well use it if you meet the requirements
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

# Grain Provinces

estate_burghers_khmer_irrigation = {
	icon = privilege_monopoly_of_goods_livestock
	influence = 0.1
	loyalty = 0.05
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } }
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 }
	}
	is_valid = {
		any_owned_province = {
			trade_goods = grain
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_khmer_irrigation }
			capital_scope = {
				trade_goods = grain
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_vaisyas_khmer_irrigation }
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_jains_khmer_irrigation }
	}
	can_select = {
		capital_scope = {
			development = 30
			trade_goods = grain
		}
		num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
			value = 10
			trade_goods = grain
			num_of_times_improved = 5
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_khmer_irrigation_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				trade_goods = grain
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_burghers_khmer_irrigation_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_khmer_irrigation_revoke_effect_tooltip
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_khmer_irrigation_mod
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_khmer_irrigation_revoke_effect_tooltip
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_khmer_irrigation_mod
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100 #might as well use it if you meet the requirements
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

# Desert Terrain/Arid Climate

estate_burghers_hydraulic_rights = {
	icon = privilege_dev_cost_desert
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -10 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	influence = 0.1
	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				has_climate = arid
				has_terrain = desert
				has_terrain = coastal_desert
			}
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_hydraulic_rights }
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					has_climate = arid
					has_terrain = desert
					has_terrain = coastal_desert
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_vaisyas_hydraulic_rights }
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_jains_hydraulic_rights }
	}
	can_select = {
		capital_scope = {
			development = 30
			OR = {
				has_terrain = desert
				has_terrain = coastal_desert
				has_climate = arid
			}
		}
		num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
			value = 10
			OR = {
				has_terrain = desert
				has_terrain = coastal_desert
				has_climate = arid
			}
			num_of_times_improved = 5
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_enslaving_rights_gt
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_terrain = desert
					has_terrain = coastal_desert
					has_climate = arid
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_burghers_hydraulic_rights_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_enslaving_rights_rt
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_hydraulic_rights_mod
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_enslaving_rights_rt
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_hydraulic_rights_mod
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100 #might as well use it if you meet the requirements
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

estate_nobles_leidang_conscription = {
	icon = privilege_sailors
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	influence = 0.05
	loyalty = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		OR = {
			has_unlocked_estate_privilege = { estate_privilege = estate_nobles_leidang_conscription }
			has_idea_group = naval_ideas
			AND = {
				has_idea_group = maritime_ideas
				has_global_modifier_value = {
					which = allowed_marine_fraction
					value = -9.75
				}
			}
		}
	}
	can_select = {
		num_of_ports = 1
	}
	modifier_by_land_ownership = {
		manpower_recovery_speed = -1
		allowed_marine_fraction = 1
	}
	on_revoked = { absolutism_revoke_effect = yes }
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes }
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0 #mostly for marine roleplaying idk
	}
}

estate_nobles_leidang_mass_conscription = {
	icon = privilege_marines
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	influence = 0.05
	loyalty = 0.05
	cooldown_years = 5
	is_valid = {
		OR = {
			has_unlocked_estate_privilege = { estate_privilege = estate_nobles_leidang_mass_conscription }
			has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_leidang_conscription
		}
	}
	can_select = {
	}
	penalties = {
		
	}
	benefits = {
		allowed_marine_fraction = 0.25
		global_sailors_modifier = 0.25
	}
	on_granted = {
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = estate_nobles_leidang_mass_conscription_mod
			duration = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_leidang_elite_conscription
			}
			remove_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_leidang_elite_conscription
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = has_no_effects_on_granted
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		remove_country_modifier = estate_nobles_leidang_mass_conscription_mod
	}
	on_revoked = {
		remove_country_modifier = estate_nobles_leidang_mass_conscription_mod
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes }
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0 #marine roleplay
	}
}

estate_burghers_orthodox_tolerance = {
	icon = privilege_tolerance_heretics
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.05
	is_valid = {
		religion_group = christian
		NOT = { religion = orthodox }
		NOT = { religion = coptic }
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				religion = orthodox
				religion = coptic
			}
		}
	}
	can_select = {
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_church_anti_heresy_act }
			remove_estate_privilege = estate_church_anti_heresy_act
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_church
				loyalty = -20
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_orthodox_tolerance_effect_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = burghers_tolerates_orthodoxy
		}
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					religion = orthodox
					religion = coptic
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_burghers_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_burghers_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_orthodox_tolerance_revoke_effect_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = burghers_tolerates_orthodoxy
		}
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_burghers_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_orthodox_tolerance_revoke_effect_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = burghers_tolerates_orthodoxy
		}
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = estate_burghers_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
			}
			remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_guaranteed_autonomy_mod
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		church_loyalty_modifier = -0.1
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes }
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOT = {
				any_owned_province = {
					NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1000
			NOT = { religious_unity = 0.5 }
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_orthodox_tolerance }
		}
		#AI will revoke this if its dominant religion is its primary religion
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			dominant_religion = ROOT
			has_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_orthodox_tolerance
			religious_unity = 0.75
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

estate_church_anti_heresy_act = {
	icon = privilege_recruit_inouisitor
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -5 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	influence = 0.1
	is_valid = {
		religion_group = christian
		NOT = { religion = orthodox }
		NOT = { religion = coptic }
		any_owned_province = {
			religion_group = ROOT
			NOT = { religion = ROOT }
		}
	}
	can_select = {
		religion_group = christian
		NOT = { religion = orthodox }
		NOT = { religion = coptic }
		any_owned_province = {
			religion_group = ROOT
			NOT = { religion = ROOT }
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_orthodox_tolerance }
			remove_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_orthodox_tolerance
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = has_no_effects_on_granted
		}
	}
	penalties = {
		burghers_loyalty_modifier = -0.05
	}
	benefits = {
		global_heretic_missionary_strength = 0.01
	}
	on_revoked = { absolutism_revoke_effect = yes }
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes }
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 21
			full_idea_group = religious_ideas
			any_owned_province = {
				religion_group = ROOT
				NOT = { religion = ROOT }
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

estate_church_religious_conscription = {
	icon = privilege_manpower_of_true_faith
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -10 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.2
	is_valid = {
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_brahmins_religious_conscription }
	}
	can_select = {
	}
	can_revoke = {
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_nobles_religious_conscription_effect_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = gets_manpower_from_tax_buildings
		}
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = ROOT
			}
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = has_building
				temple = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = estate_nobles_religious_conscription_temple
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				cathedral = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = estate_nobles_religious_conscription_cathedral
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				grand_treasury = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = estate_nobles_religious_conscription_grand_treasury
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			remove_province_modifier = estate_nobles_religious_conscription_cathedral
			remove_province_modifier = estate_nobles_religious_conscription_grand_treasury
			remove_province_modifier = estate_nobles_religious_conscription_temple
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_nobles_religious_conscription_revoke_effect_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = gets_manpower_from_tax_buildings
		}
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = estate_nobles_religious_conscription_cathedral
		remove_province_modifier = estate_nobles_religious_conscription_grand_treasury
		remove_province_modifier = estate_nobles_religious_conscription_temple
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_nobles_religious_conscription_revoke_effect_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = gets_manpower_from_tax_buildings
		}
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = estate_nobles_religious_conscription_cathedral
		remove_province_modifier = estate_nobles_religious_conscription_grand_treasury
		remove_province_modifier = estate_nobles_religious_conscription_temple
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes }
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 20
		modifier = {
			factor = 0 # This privilege is good, but increases influence so be careful if you havent completed court and country
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_church_religious_conscription }
			estate_influence = {
				estate = estate_church
				influence = 45
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOT = {
				num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
					value = 10
					has_tax_building_trigger = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
