		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_tribe_unification }
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_tribe_centralization }
	}
	on_revoked = { absolutism_revoke_effect = yes } can_revoke = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = estate_nobles_decentralized_tribe_tt
			has_country_flag = centralized_tribes_level_2
		}
		absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes
	}
	modifier_by_land_ownership = {
		nobles_loyalty_modifier = 0.2
		land_forcelimit_modifier = 0.2
		manpower_recovery_speed = 0.15
		global_autonomy = 0.05
	}
	mechanics = {
		exempt_from_seize_land
	}
	on_granted = {
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_nobles
			loyalty = 5
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = centralized_tribes_level_1
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0
	}
}

estate_nobles_tribe_unification = {
	icon = privilege_unifying
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -10 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	influence = 0.05
	loyalty = 0
	is_valid = {
		has_government_attribute = has_internal_tribes
		has_country_flag = centralized_tribes_level_1
	}
	can_select = {
		legitimacy = 90
		NOT = { num_of_rebel_controlled_provinces = 1 }
		NOT = { num_of_rebel_armies = 1 }
		estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_nobles
			loyalty = 70
		}
		stability = 2
	}
	modifier_by_land_ownership = {
		nobles_loyalty_modifier = 0.1
		land_forcelimit_modifier = 0.1
		manpower_recovery_speed = 0.075
		global_autonomy = 0.025
	}
	benefits = {
		legitimacy = 0.25
	}
	on_granted = {
		set_country_flag = estate_nobles_tribe_unification_flag
		tooltip = {
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_nobles
				loyalty = -40
			}
			add_stability = -1
			remove_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_decentralized_tribe
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = centralized_tribes_level_2
			country_event = {
				id = flavor_jol.100
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked = { absolutism_revoke_effect = yes } 
	can_revoke = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = estate_nobles_tribe_unification_tt
			has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_tribe_centralization
		}
		absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes
	}
	mechanics = {
		exempt_from_seize_land
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1000
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_country_flag = estate_nobles_tribe_unification_flag
		}
	}
}

		}
		stability = 2
	}

		tooltip = {
			add_stability = -2

				loyalty = -50
			}
			change_government_to_monarchy = yes
			remove_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_tribe_unification
			remove_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_tribe_centralization
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = centralized_tribes_level_1
			clr_country_flag = centralized_tribes_level_2
			set_country_flag = centralized_tribes_level_3
			country_event = {
				id = flavor_jol.101
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked = { absolutism_revoke_effect = yes } 
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1000
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_country_flag = estate_nobles_tribe_centralization_flag
		}
	}
}

estate_dhimmi_alm_black_gold = {
	icon = privilege_monopoly_of_goods_dyes
	conditional_modifier = { 
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country } } 
		modifier = { max_absolutism = -15 } 
		is_bad = yes 
	}
	loyalty = 0.05
	influence = 0.1
	land_share = 5
	is_valid = {
		any_owned_province = {
			trade_goods = coffee
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_alm_granted_black_gold_tooltip
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = estate_burghers_alm_black_gold }
	}
	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				trade_goods = coffee
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_burghers_alm_black_gold
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = {
			remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_alm_black_gold
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_alm_revoked_black_gold_tooltip
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = estate_burghers_alm_black_gold }
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_alm_black_gold
	}
	on_invalid = {
		custom_tooltip = estate_burghers_alm_revoked_black_gold_tooltip
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = estate_burghers_alm_black_gold }
	}
	on_invalid_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_alm_black_gold
	}
	penalties = {
	}
	benefits = {
	}
	can_revoke = { absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes } 
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 5
				trade_goods = coffee
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { is_absolutism_active = yes }
					NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_dhimmi_alm_black_gold }
					NOT = { crown_land_share = 20 }
				}
				AND = {
					is_absolutism_active = yes
					NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_dhimmi_alm_black_gold }
					NOT = { crown_land_share = 60 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}

			custom_trigger_tooltip = {

				has_country_flag = eoc_resolved_miao_revolts
			}
		}
		else = {
			always = yes
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		custom_tooltip = shen_provinces_modifier_tt
		hidden_effect = {

		custom_tooltip = remove_shen_provinces_modifier_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = eunuchs_harmonize_folk_religions_mod }
				remove_province_modifier = eunuchs_harmonize_folk_religions_mod
			}
		}
	}
	on_invalid = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = eunuchs_harmonize_folk_religions_mod }
				remove_province_modifier = eunuchs_harmonize_folk_religions_mod
			}
		}
	}
	conditional_modifier = {

		is_bad = yes
	}

		factor = 1

			factor = 0
			OR = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
							value = 10
							religion = shen
						}
					}
					NOT = { dominant_religion = shen }
				}
				AND = {
					is_absolutism_active = yes
					NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
				}
				AND = {
					religious_unity = 0.9
					has_estate_privilege = estate_eunuchs_harmonize_folk_religions
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			OR = {

				dominant_religion = shen
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0

			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }

	on_granted_province = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { religion = ROOT } }
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = sufi_autonomy_modifier
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				religion = ROOT 
				has_province_modifier = sufi_autonomy_modifier
			}
			remove_province_modifier = sufi_autonomy_modifier
		}
	}
	on_revoked_province = {
		remove_province_modifier = sufi_autonomy_modifier
	}
	penalties = {
		global_autonomy = 0.5
	}
	mechanics = {
		exempt_from_seize_land
	}
	is_valid = {
		has_estate_privilege = estate_church_tim_sufi_autonomy
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 0
	}
}
estate_eunuchs_national_recovery = {
	icon = privilege_admin_power
	influence = 0.2
	loyalty = 0.05

	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
		modifier = {
			max_absolutism = -15
		}
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = { ai = no }
		modifier = {
			infantry_power = -0.15
		}
	}
	conditional_modifier = {
		trigger = { ai = yes }
		modifier = {
			imperial_mandate = 0.05
			global_monthly_devastation = -0.5
			country_military_power = 3
			country_admin_power = 3
			country_diplomatic_power = 3
		}
	}
	on_granted = {
		if = {
			limit = { ai = no }
			custom_tooltip = player_lose_devastation_in_provinces
			hidden_effect = {
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						devastation = 10
					}
					add_devastation = -10
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = ai_lose_devastation_in_provinces
			hidden_effect = {
				every_owned_province = {
					add_devastation = -20
				}
			}
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = imperial_mandate
				0 = {
					add_mandate = 40
				}
				20 = {
					add_mandate = 25
				}
				40 = {
					add_mandate = 10
				}
				60 = {
					add_mandate = 5
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = eunuchs_recovery_flag
	}
	benefits = {
		global_monthly_devastation = -1
		global_prosperity_growth = 2
	}
	penalties = {
		country_military_power = -5
		country_admin_power = -5
		country_diplomatic_power = -5
	}
	can_revoke = {
		absolutism_can_revoke_trigger = yes
		if = {
			limit = { ai = no }
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = "Had this privilege active for at least 10 years."
				had_country_flag = {
					flag = eunuchs_recovery_flag
					days = 3650
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = "Had this privilege active for at least 5 years."
				had_country_flag = {
					flag = eunuchs_recovery_flag
					days = 1825
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_revoked = {
		absolutism_revoke_effect = yes
		clr_country_flag = eunuchs_recovery_flag
	}
	on_invalid = {
		clr_country_flag = eunuchs_recovery_flag
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 5
				devastation = 10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				devastation = 10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 5
				devastation = 20
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				devastation = 20
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 5
				devastation = 30
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				devastation = 30
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1000
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 2
				devastation = 50
			}
			NOT = { imperial_mandate = 50 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			NOT = { imperial_mandate = 30 }
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				devastation = 10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			NOT = { imperial_mandate = 1 }
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 5
				devastation = 10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			imperial_mandate = 75
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_absolutism_active = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = resolved_court_and_country }
		}
	}
}
